[ 2710s]     def invoke_exception_view(
[ 2710s]         self, exc_info=None, request=None, secure=True, reraise=False
[ 2710s]     ):
[ 2710s]         """Executes an exception view related to the request it's called upon.
[ 2710s]         The arguments it takes are these:
[ 2710s]     
[ 2710s]         ``exc_info``
[ 2710s]     
[ 2710s]             If provided, should be a 3-tuple in the form provided by
[ 2710s]             ``sys.exc_info()``.  If not provided,
[ 2710s]             ``sys.exc_info()`` will be called to obtain the current
[ 2710s]             interpreter exception information.  Default: ``None``.
[ 2710s]     
[ 2710s]         ``request``
[ 2710s]     
[ 2710s]             If the request to be used is not the same one as the instance that
[ 2710s]             this method is called upon, it may be passed here.  Default:
[ 2710s]             ``None``.
[ 2710s]     
[ 2710s]         ``secure``
[ 2710s]     
[ 2710s]             If the exception view should not be rendered if the current user
[ 2710s]             does not have the appropriate permission, this should be ``True``.
[ 2710s]             Default: ``True``.
[ 2710s]     
[ 2710s]         ``reraise``
[ 2710s]     
[ 2710s]             A boolean indicating whether the original error should be reraised
[ 2710s]             if a :term:`response` object could not be created. If ``False``
[ 2710s]             then an :class:`pyramid.httpexceptions.HTTPNotFound`` exception
[ 2710s]             will be raised. Default: ``False``.
[ 2710s]     
[ 2710s]         If a response is generated then ``request.exception`` and
[ 2710s]         ``request.exc_info`` will be left at the values used to render the
[ 2710s]         response. Otherwise the previous values for ``request.exception`` and
[ 2710s]         ``request.exc_info`` will be restored.
[ 2710s]     
[ 2710s]         .. versionadded:: 1.7
[ 2710s]     
[ 2710s]         .. versionchanged:: 1.9
[ 2710s]            The ``request.exception`` and ``request.exc_info`` properties will
[ 2710s]            reflect the exception used to render the response where previously
[ 2710s]            they were reset to the values prior to invoking the method.
[ 2710s]     
[ 2710s]            Also added the ``reraise`` argument.
[ 2710s]     
[ 2710s]         """
[ 2710s]         if request is None:
[ 2710s]             request = self
[ 2710s]         registry = getattr(request, 'registry', None)
[ 2710s]         if registry is None:
[ 2710s]             registry = get_current_registry()
[ 2710s]     
[ 2710s]         if registry is None:

[ 2710s]

[ 2710s]

[ 2710s]         attrs = request.__dict__
[ 2710s]         context_iface = providedBy(exc)
[ 2710s]
